44	(** A low byte and a high-shifted value share no bits. *)
45	Lemma land_lo_hi : forall a b, 0 <= a < 256 -> 0 <= b -> Z.land a (b * 256) = 0.
46	Proof.
47	  intros a b Ha Hb. apply Z.bits_inj'. intros i Hi.
48	  rewrite Z.land_spec, Z.bits_0.
49	  replace (b * 256) with (Z.shiftl b 8) by (rewrite Z.shiftl_mul_pow2 by lia; change (2^8) with 256; ring).
50	  destruct (i <? 8) eqn:E.
51	  - apply Z.ltb_lt in E. rewrite Z.shiftl_spec_low by lia. apply andb_false_r.

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  00:05:17; tool 6ms

```
1	(** * A minimal, executable RV64I model in Coq -- mirror of lean/Hex0/Rv64i.lean.
2	
3	    Same 12 instruction encodings used by bare/core.s:
4	      ADDI ADD OR SLLI LBU SB BEQ BLT BGE BGEU JAL JALR
5	    64-bit words are [Z] kept in [0, 2^64); operations wrap explicitly. Memory
6	    is byte-addressed ([Z -> Z], bytes in [0,256)). The model computes under
7	    [vm_compute] so it can be run on the real binary bytes (see Validate.v). *)
8	
9	From Coq Require Import ZArith List Lia Bool.
10	Import ListNotations.
11	Local Open Scope Z_scope.
12	
13	Definition w64 : Z := 2 ^ 64.
14	
15	Definition wrap (z : Z) : Z := z mod w64.
16	Definition wadd (a b : Z) : Z := wrap (a + b).
17	Definition wor  (a b : Z) : Z := Z.lor a b.
18	Definition wshl (a : Z) (n : Z) : Z := wrap (Z.shiftl a n).
19	
20	(* sign-extend a [k]-bit raw value to a (possibly negative) Z *)
21	Definition sext (k raw : Z) : Z :=
22	  if raw >=? 2 ^ (k - 1) then raw - 2 ^ k else raw.
23	
24	(* unsigned / signed comparisons on in-range words *)
25	Definition toS (x : Z) : Z := if x >=? 2 ^ 63 then x - w64 else x.
26	Definition ultb (a b : Z) : bool := a <? b.
27	Definition sltb (a b : Z) : bool := toS a <? toS b.
28	
29	(* extract [len] bits at offset [lo] from a 32-bit value *)
30	Definition field (w lo len : Z) : Z := (w / 2 ^ lo) mod 2 ^ len.
31	
32	Record State := mkState {
33	  reg : Z -> Z;     (* x0..x31 ; x0 forced to 0 by rget/rset *)
34	  pc  : Z;
35	  mem : Z -> Z      (* byte-addressed *)
36	}.
37	
38	Definition rget (s : State) (i : Z) : Z := if i =? 0 then 0 else s.(reg) i.
39	
40	Definition rset (s : State) (i : Z) (v : Z) : State :=
41	  if i =? 0 then s
42	  else mkState (fun j => if j =? i then v else s.(reg) j) s.(pc) s.(mem).
43	
44	Definition setPc (s : State) (p : Z) : State := mkState s.(reg) p s.(mem).
45	
46	Definition storeByte (s : State) (a b : Z) : State :=
47	  mkState s.(reg) s.(pc) (fun x => if x =? a then b mod 256 else s.(mem) x).
48	
49	Definition fetch32 (s : State) : Z :=
50	  let b0 := s.(mem) s.(pc) in
51	  let b1 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 1) in
52	  let b2 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 2) in
53	  let b3 := s.(mem) (s.(pc) + 3) in
54	  b0 + b1 * 256 + b2 * 65536 + b3 * 16777216.
55	
56	Inductive Instr :=
57	  | Iaddi (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
58	  | Iadd  (rd rs1 rs2 : Z)
59	  | Ior   (rd rs1 rs2 : Z)
60	  | Islli (rd rs1 : Z) (shamt : Z)
61	  | Ilbu  (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
62	  | Isb   (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
63	  | Ibeq  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
64	  | Iblt  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
65	  | Ibge  (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
66	  | Ibgeu (rs1 rs2 : Z) (imm : Z)
67	  | Ijal  (rd : Z) (imm : Z)
68	  | Ijalr (rd rs1 : Z) (imm : Z)
69	  | Iunknown.
70	
71	(* immediates are stored as sign-extended Z, ready to feed into wadd *)
72	Definition decode (w : Z) : Instr :=
73	  let opcode := field w 0 7 in
74	  let rd     := field w 7 5 in
75	  let funct3 := field w 12 3 in
76	  let rs1    := field w 15 5 in
77	  let rs2    := field w 20 5 in
78	  let funct7 := field w 25 7 in
79	  let immI   := sext 12 (field w 20 12) in
80	  let shamt  := field w 20 6 in
81	  let immS   := sext 12 (Z.lor (Z.shiftl funct7 5) rd) in
82	  let immB   := sext 13 (Z.lor (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 31 1) 12) (Z.shiftl (field w 7 1) 11))
83	                               (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 25 6) 5) (Z.shiftl (field w 8 4) 1))) in
84	  let immJ   := sext 21 (Z.lor (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 31 1) 20) (Z.shiftl (field w 12 8) 12))
85	                               (Z.lor (Z.shiftl (field w 20 1) 11) (Z.shiftl (field w 21 10) 1))) in
86	  if opcode =? 19 then            (* 0x13 OP-IMM *)
87	    if funct3 =? 0 then Iaddi rd rs1 immI
88	    else if funct3 =? 1 then (if funct7 =? 0 then Islli rd rs1 shamt else Iunknown)
89	    else Iunknown
90	  else if opcode =? 51 then       (* 0x33 OP *)
91	    if funct7 =? 0 then
92	      (if funct3 =? 0 then Iadd rd rs1 rs2
93	       else if funct3 =? 6 then Ior rd rs1 rs2 else Iunknown)
94	    else Iunknown
95	  else if opcode =? 3 then        (* 
… [truncated 2321 chars]

2	
3	This is the plan for the **last open item** in the hex0 verification tower: removing

9	methodology). Everything *above* the ISA layer (`core_refines`, grammar,
10	certification) is already proved in both Lean and Coq; this is the floor of the
11	tower.
12	
13	---
14	
15	## 0. Status of this task after recon (2026-06-02)
16	
17	**The oracle is already installed and the cross-check empirically holds on the
18	real binary.** Concretely:
19	
20	- The opam switch (`~/.opam/CP.2025.01.0~8.20~2025.01`) ships **`coq-riscv.0.0.5`**
21	  (the MIT **riscv-coq** / *riscv-semantics* model — the spec used by
22	  bedrock2/`compiler`, generated by `hs-to-coq` from the official Haskell
23	  `riscv-semantics`) plus its deps **`coq-coqutil.0.0.6`** (`word`, `map`).
24	  Path: `~/.opam/.../lib/coq/user-contrib/riscv/` (on Coq's default load path —
25	  `Require Import riscv.Spec.Decode.` just works; verified).
26	- All **12** instruction forms `core` uses exist in riscv-coq's `InstructionI`
27	  (`Addi Add Or Slli Lbu Sb Beq Blt Bge Bgeu Jal Jalr`).
28	- **Empirical differential already run and PASSED** (`/tmp/cross_diff.v`, reproduced
29	  below): decoding every one of the **81** instruction words of the real `core`
30	  image both ways agrees **field-for-field** (opcode, rd/rs1/rs2, every immediate),
31	  and our model decodes **0** of them to `Iunknown`. So on the actual deployed
32	  bytes, our decoder = riscv-coq's decoder, exactly.
33	
34	  ```
35	  Eval vm_compute in (allAgree 81).   (* = true  *)
36	  Eval vm_compute in (cntUnknown 81). (* = 0     *)
37	  ```
38	
39	What remains is to turn that empirical agreement into **theorems** (general over
40	all 32-bit words for decode; over the 12 forms under a state-bridge for execute),
41	which is what actually discharges the TCB obligation.
42

44	
45	`decode_agrees` is **proved, `Admitted`-free, and closed under the global context
46	(ZERO axioms)** — kernel-checked, built by `make` in the pipeline:
47	
48	```coq
49	Theorem decode_agrees : forall w, 0 <= w < 2 ^ 32 ->
50	  forall i, Rv64i.decode w = i -> i <> Iunknown -> Decode.decode RV64I w = embed i.
51	```
52	
53	`Print Assumptions decode_agrees` ⇒ *Closed under the global context*. So for **every**
54	32-bit word, whenever our decoder yields one of the 12 modelled instructions,
55	riscv-coq's `decode RV64I` yields the corresponding instruction with identical
56	operands. **Our decoder is no longer trusted — it is proved equal to the reference
57	decoder.** Proof structure actually used (≈300 lines):
58	- bridges `field_bitSlice` (`field = bitSlice`), `sext_signExtend` (on in-range inputs);
59	- range toolkit `field_lt`/`lor_lt`/`shiftl_field_lt` + `range_tac` (immediate bounds),
60	  `field_sub0` (subfield-of-zero, for SLLI's funct6/shamtHi from funct7=0);
61	- per-form lemmas `decode_addi/slli/add/or/lbu/sb/beq/blt/bge/bgeu/jal/jalr`, each:
62	  rewrite control fields → `cbn` riscv-coq's decode control-flow (operands kept abstract
63	  via `Opaque bitSlice signExtend Z.shiftl Z.lor`) → convert operands → close the

66	  contradicts the hypothesis). The SLLI `shamt≥32` gap (§5) does **not** affect T1 —
67	  it only concerns the reverse direction.

Definition execute {p : Type -> Type} {t : Type} `{Spec.Machine.RiscvMachine p
                                                                             t}
   : Spec.Decode.InstructionI -> p unit :=
  fun arg_0__ =>
    match arg_0__ with
    | Spec.Decode.Lui rd imm20 =>
        Spec.Machine.setRegister rd (Utility.Utility.fromImm imm20)
    | Spec.Decode.Auipc rd oimm20 =>
        Bind Spec.Machine.getPC (fun pc =>
                Spec.Machine.setRegister rd (Utility.Utility.fromImm oimm20 + pc))

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  00:05:36; tool 11ms

```
134	(* The embedding of our [Instr] into riscv-coq's [Instruction], and    *)
135	(* the per-instruction decode-agreement lemmas.                        *)
136	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
137	
138	Definition embed (i : Rv64i.Instr) : Instruction :=
139	  match i with
140	  | Iaddi rd rs1 imm => IInstruction (Addi rd rs1 imm)
141	  | Iadd  rd rs1 rs2 => IInstruction (Add  rd rs1 rs2)
142	  | Ior   rd rs1 rs2 => IInstruction (Or   rd rs1 rs2)
143	  | Islli rd rs1 sh  => IInstruction (Slli rd rs1 sh)
144	  | Ilbu  rd rs1 imm => IInstruction (Lbu  rd rs1 imm)
145	  | Isb   rs1 rs2 imm=> IInstruction (Sb   rs1 rs2 imm)
146	  | Ibeq  rs1 rs2 imm=> IInstruction (Beq  rs1 rs2 imm)
147	  | Iblt  rs1 rs2 imm=> IInstruction (Blt  rs1 rs2 imm)
148	  | Ibge  rs1 rs2 imm=> IInstruction (Bge  rs1 rs2 imm)
149	  | Ibgeu rs1 rs2 imm=> IInstruction (Bgeu rs1 rs2 imm)
150	  | Ijal  rd imm     => IInstruction (Jal  rd imm)
151	  | Ijalr rd rs1 imm => IInstruction (Jalr rd rs1 imm)
152	  | Iunknown         => InvalidInstruction 0
153	  end.
154	
155	(* Keep these abstract so [cbn] reduces only riscv-coq's decode CONTROL flow,
156	   leaving the operands as clean bitSlice/signExtend/shiftl/lor terms. *)
157	Opaque bitSlice signExtend Z.shiftl Z.lor.
158	
159	(** Convert our [field]/[sext] operands to riscv-coq form and close by the
160	    decode/encode bit-equality prover. Handles all 12 forms uniformly. *)
161	Ltac finish w :=
162	  rewrite ?(sext_signExtend _) by (try lia; range_tac);
163	  rewrite !(f_bs w _ _) by lia;
164	  f_equal; f_equal; with_strategy transparent [bitSlice] prove_Zeq_bitwise.
165	
166	Lemma decode_addi : forall w,
167	  Rv64i.field w 0 7 = 19 -> Rv64i.field w 12 3 = 0 ->
168	  decode RV64I w = embed (Iaddi (Rv64i.field w 7 5) (Rv64i.field w 15 5) (Rv64i.sext 12 (Rv64i.field w 20 12))).
```

300	(* T1: decode agreement, for every 32-bit word.                        *)
301	(* ------------------------------------------------------------------ *)
302	
303	(** Whenever our decoder returns one of the 12 modelled instructions, riscv-coq's
304	    [decode RV64I] returns the corresponding instruction with identical operands. *)
305	Theorem decode_agrees : forall w, 0 <= w < 2 ^ 32 ->
306	  forall i, Rv64i.decode w = i -> i <> Iunknown -> decode RV64I w = embed i.
307	Proof.
308	  intros w Hw i Hi Hni. subst i. unfold Rv64i.decode in *.
309	  set (op := Rv64i.field w 0 7) in *.
310	  set (f3 := Rv64i.field w 12 3) in *.
311	  set (f7 := Rv64i.field w 25 7) in *.
312	  destruct (op =? 19) eqn:E19.
313	  - apply Z.eqb_eq in E19. destruct (f3 =? 0) eqn:Ef0.
314	    + apply Z.eqb_eq in Ef0. apply decode_addi; assumption.

323	        -- apply Z.eqb_eq in Ef0. apply decode_add; assumption.
324	        -- destruct (f3 =? 6) eqn:Ef6.
325	           ++ apply Z.eqb_eq in Ef6. apply decode_or; assumption.
326	           ++ exfalso; apply Hni; reflexivity.
327	      * exfalso; apply Hni; reflexivity.
328	    + destruct (op =? 3) eqn:E3.
329	      * apply Z.eqb_eq in E3. destruct (f3 =? 4) eqn:Ef4.

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  00:31:24; tool 96ms

```
=== alu_scope notations and MachineWidth class ===
Class MachineWidth(t: Type) := {

  (* arithmetic operations (inherited from wegral in Haskell) *)
  add: t -> t -> t;
  sub: t -> t -> t;
  mul: t -> t -> t;
  div: t -> t -> t;
  rem: t -> t -> t;

  negate: t -> t;

  (* comparison operators *)
  reg_eqb: t -> t -> bool;
  signed_less_than: t -> t -> bool;
  ltu: t -> t -> bool;

  (* logical operations (inherited from Bits in Haskell) *)
  xor: t -> t -> t;
  or: t -> t -> t;
  and: t -> t -> t;

  (* bitwidth of type t: *)
  XLEN: Z;

  (* operations also defined in MachineWidth in Haskell: *)

  regToInt8: t -> w8;
  regToInt16: t -> w16;
  regToInt32: t -> w32;
  regToInt64: t -> w64;

  uInt8ToReg: w8 -> t;
  uInt16ToReg: w16 -> t;
  uInt32ToReg: w32 -> t;
  uInt64ToReg: w64 -> t;

  int8ToReg: w8 -> t;
  int16ToReg: w16 -> t;
  int32ToReg: w32 -> t;
  int64ToReg: w64 -> t;

  s32: t -> t;
  u32: t -> t;

  regToZ_signed: t -> Z;
  regToZ_unsigned: t -> Z;

  sll: t -> Z -> t;
  srl: t -> Z -> t;
  sra: t -> Z -> t;

  divu: t -> t -> t;
  remu: t -> t -> t;

  maxSigned: t;
  maxUnsigned: t;
  minSigned: t;

  regToShamt5: t -> Z;
  regToShamt: t -> Z;

  highBits: Z -> t;

  (* additional conversions: *)
  ZToReg: Z -> t;
}.

Notation fromImm := (@ZToReg _ _) (only parsing).

Section Derived.

  Context {t: Type}.
  Context {MW: MachineWidth t}.

  Definition XLEN_in_bytes: Z := XLEN / 8.

  Definition lnot(x: t): t := xor x maxUnsigned.

End Derived.

Declare Scope alu_scope.

Notation "a <|> b" := (or a b)  (at level 50, left associativity) : alu_scope.
Notation "a <&> b" := (and a b) (at level 40, left associativity) : alu_scope.
Notation "a + b"   := (add a b) (at level 50, left associativity) : alu_scope.
Notation "a - b"   := (sub a b) (at level 50, left associativity) : alu_scope.
Notation "a * b"   := (mul a b) (at level 40, left associativity) : alu_scope.

22	    tuple.unfoldn (fun w => word.add w (word.of_Z 1)) sz a.
23	
24	  Definition load_bytes(sz: nat)(m: mem)(addr: word): option (tuple byte sz) :=
25	    map.getmany_of_tuple m (footprint addr sz).

28	    map.putmany_of_tuple (footprint a sz) bs m.

31	    match load_bytes sz m a with
32	    | Some _ => Some (unchecked_store_bytes sz m a v)
33	    | None => None (* some addresses were invalid *)
34	    end.

### 🛠️ **Tool result**  ·  00:38:50; tool 90ms

```
Definition encodePrivMode(m: PrivMode): MachineInt :=
  match m with
  | User => 0
  | Supervisor => 1
  | Machine => 3
  end.

Definition PrivMode_eqb(m1 m2: PrivMode): bool := Z.eqb (encodePrivMode m1) (encodePrivMode m2).

Definition PrivMode_ltb(m1 m2: PrivMode): bool := Z.ltb (encodePrivMode m1) (encodePrivMode m2).

Inductive AccessType: Set := Instr | Load | Store.
Inductive SourceType: Set := VirtualMemory | Fetch | Execute.

Class RiscvProgram{M}{t}`{Monad M}`{MachineWidth t} := mkRiscvProgram {
  getRegister: Register -> M t;
  setRegister: Register -> t -> M unit;

  loadByte   : SourceType -> t -> M w8;
  loadHalf   : SourceType -> t -> M w16;
  loadWord   : SourceType -> t -> M w32;
  loadDouble : SourceType -> t -> M w64;

  storeByte   : SourceType -> t -> w8 -> M unit;
  storeHalf   : SourceType -> t -> w16 -> M unit;
  storeWord   : SourceType -> t -> w32 -> M unit;
  storeDouble : SourceType -> t -> w64 -> M unit;

  makeReservation  : t -> M unit;
  clearReservation : t -> M unit;
  checkReservation : t -> M bool;

  getCSRField : CSRField -> M MachineInt;
  setCSRField : CSRField -> MachineInt -> M unit;

  getPC: M t;
  setPC: t -> M unit;
  getPrivMode: M PrivMode;
  setPrivMode: PrivMode -> M unit;
  fence: MachineInt -> MachineInt -> M unit;

  (* Both of these update the PC at the end of a cycle.
     Every instance must support endCycleNormal.
     All operations following endCycleEarly are skipped.
     Some instances may not support endCycleEarly and fail instead. *)
  endCycleNormal: M unit;
  endCycleEarly: forall A, M A;
}.


Class RiscvMachine`{MP: RiscvProgram} := mkRiscvMachine {
  (* checks that addr is aligned, and translates the (possibly virtual) addr to a physical
     address, raising an exception if the address is invalid *)
  translate(accessType: AccessType)(alignment: t)(addr: t): M t;
  flushTLB: M unit;
  getCSR_InstRet: M MachineInt;
Shell cwd was reset to /var/data/bootstrap
```

3226:Theorem init_loopinv : forall inp cap, WellFormed inp cap ->
3227:  LoopInv inp cap (runUntil 0 2 (mkInit (Z.of_nat (length inp)) cap (memWith inp inputAddr))) inp [].
3230:  set (init := mkInit (Z.of_nat (length inp)) cap (memWith inp inputAddr)).

3298:  WellFormed inp cap ->
3304:  pose proof (init_loopinv inp cap HW) as HLI.
3305:  set (init := mkInit (Z.of_nat (length inp)) cap (memWith inp inputAddr)) in *.
3306:  pose proof (loop_correct inp cap (length inp) inp [] (runUntil 0 2 init) (le_n _) HLI) as HR.

### 🤖 **Assistant**  ·  01:14:29; model 14.7s

Done. Here's where task #7 stands now.

## What I accomplished this session

**Proved `step_agrees`** — the full execute/step cross-check (T2) of our `Rv64i.step` against riscv-coq's `Run.run1 RV64I` over the Minimal `OState` machine. It's in the new `coq/RvCrossExec.v` (880 lines), `Admitted`-free, and `Print Assumptions step_agrees` reports only `functional_extensionality_dep` (the same standard axiom the rest of the dev and coqutil/riscv already use).

```coq
Theorem step_agrees : forall s (m:RMach) D,
  Rrel s m D -> WFstep s m D ->
  Rv64i.decode (Rv64i.fetch32 s) <> Iunknown ->
  exists m', Run.run1 RV64I m = (Some tt, m') /\ Rrel (Rv64i.step s) m' D.
```

Under the state bridge `Rrel` and the §5 side conditions `WFstep` (branch/jump targets 4-aligned; `lbu`/`sb` data address in the tracked domain — all true of the loaded `core`), **one of our steps computes exactly one riscv-coq cycle, succeeding and landing in a related state.**

All **12** per-instruction lemmas are proved (`exec_addi/add/or/slli/lbu/sb/beq/blt/bge/bgeu/jal/jalr`), each via: fetch → `run1` reduce → `decode_agrees` (T1) → reduce `ExecuteI` through the word/memory bridges → reassemble `Rrel`. Differences the cross-check now turns into *theorems* rather than assumptions: SLLI `shamt<32` narrowing, the misaligned-target exception, the JALR bit-0 clear (`clearbit0: Z.land a (2^64-2) = a - a mod 2`), x0 semantics, register-index validity, and fetch/data-domain conditions.

The whole Coq dev rebuilds green from clean.

## What remains

Only the **transport corollary `core_refines_riscv`**: lift `step_agrees` over a full run by induction (mirroring `loop_correct`), add a prologue relating riscv's init machine to our `mkInit` by `Rrel`, and compose with the finished `core_refines`. This is a sizable, separate integration with `Refine.v`'s internals — I deliberately stopped at the verified `step_agrees` boundary rather than start that large piece at the tail of a long session. I documented the plan and all the gotchas in `RESUME.md`.

Committed on `isa-crosscheck-decode` as `bda1f29`, with `STATUS.md` / `CROSSCHECK.md` / `RESUME.md` updated.
